<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Introductory Note</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All of the information contained in this Form&nbsp;8-K relates to the previously announced sale by Target Corporation (&#147;Target&#148;) of its entire consumer credit card portfolio to The Toronto-Dominion Bank (&#147;TD&#148;), which was completed on March&nbsp;13, 2013 (the &#147;Transaction&#148;) and is discussed in more detail under Item 2.01. </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As disclosed in the News Release attached to this Form&nbsp;8-K, on March&nbsp;13, 2013, Target also announced the commencement of tender offers to use up to an aggregate of $1.2 billion of cash proceeds from the Transaction to repurchase outstanding debt and, over time, Target expects to apply the remaining proceeds from the Transaction to further reduce its debt position and continue its current share repurchase program. The pro forma financial statements included with this Form&nbsp;8-K do not reflect the full application of the proceeds from the Transaction and therefore are not indicative of the financial impact of this Transaction. Following the completion of the debt tender offer, Target will provide updated forward-looking information that will include the full expected impact of the Transaction and related application of proceeds, as well as comparative historical results for its U.S. Segment (formerly the U.S. Retail and U.S. Credit Card Segments).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1.01.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement</font></u></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a result of the closing of the Transaction on March&nbsp;13, 2013, pursuant to the Credit Card Program Agreement, dated as of October&nbsp;22, 2012, between Target, its wholly-owned subsidiary, Target Enterprise,&nbsp;Inc., and TD Bank USA, N.A., an affiliate of TD (the &#147;Credit Card Program Agreement&#148;), TD&#146;s rights and obligations to underwrite, fund and own Target Credit Card and Target Visa receivables in the U.S. became effective and the seven-year term of the Credit Card Program Agreement began. In addition to those rights and obligations under the Credit Card Program Agreement, TD controls risk management policies and oversees regulatory compliance. Target performs account servicing and primary marketing functions, and earns a substantial portion of the profits generated by the Target Credit Card and Target Visa portfolios.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A copy of the Credit Card Program Agreement will be filed as an Exhibit&nbsp;to Target&#146;s Quarterly Report on Form&nbsp;10-Q for the quarter ending May&nbsp;4, 2013.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1.02.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Termination of a Material Definitive Agreement</font></u></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On March&nbsp;13, 2013, Target terminated its Amended and Restated Pooling and Servicing Agreement, dated as of April&nbsp;28, 2000, among Target Receivables LLC (formerly known as Target Receivables Corporation), Target National Bank (formerly known as Retailers National Bank) and Wells Fargo Bank, National Association (formerly known as Wells Fargo Bank Minnesota, National Association), as previously amended, including most recently as of January&nbsp;26, 2012 (the &#147;Pooling and Servicing Agreement&#148;). The Pooling and Servicing Agreement contained provisions related to the conveyance of credit card receivables by Target Receivables LLC to the Target Credit Card Master Trust, the administration and servicing of the receivables, and the rights of the certificate holders in the Target Credit Card Master Trust. The Pooling and Servicing Agreement was terminated in connection with the Transaction.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.01.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets</font></u></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On March&nbsp;13, 2013, Target completed the previously announced sale of its entire consumer credit card portfolio to TD pursuant to the Purchase and Sale Agreement, dated as of October&nbsp;22, 2012, between Target, two of its wholly owned subsidiaries, Target Receivables LLC and Target National Bank, and TD Bank USA, N.A., an affiliate of TD, as amended (the &#147;Purchase and Sale Agreement&#148;). The purchase price for the Transaction is approximately $5.7 billion, and is equal to the gross value of the outstanding receivables at the time of closing. Concurrent with the Transaction, Target repaid </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the nonrecourse debt collateralized by credit card receivables (2006/2007 Series&nbsp;Variable Funding Certificate) for approximately $1.5 billion, equal to par, resulting in net cash proceeds of approximately $4.2 billion.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A copy of the News Release announcing the completion of the Transaction is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;(99). The Purchase and Sale Agreement was filed </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">as an Exhibit&nbsp;to Target&#146;s Quarterly Report on Form&nbsp;10-Q for the quarter ended October&nbsp;27, 2012. The First Amendment to the Purchase and Sale Agreement is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;(2)G.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 9.01.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial Statements and Exhibits</font></u></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(b)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro forma financial information</font></u></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following unaudited pro forma consolidated financial statements are based on the consolidated financial statements of Target, and are adjusted to give effect to Transaction under the Purchase and Sale Agreement and the rights and obligations under the related Program Agreement as if the Transaction occurred at an earlier date. As specified in Article&nbsp;11 of Regulation S-X, the unaudited pro forma Consolidated Statements of Operations for fiscal year 2011 and the nine months ended October&nbsp;27, 2012 are adjusted to reflect the Transaction as if it occurred on January&nbsp;30, 2011. The unaudited pro forma Consolidated Statement of Financial Position is adjusted to reflect the Transaction as if it occurred on October&nbsp;27, 2012, the last day of the most recently filed period.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The unaudited pro forma consolidated financial statements are presented for illustrative purposes only and, therefore, are not indicative of the operating results and financial position that might have been achieved had the Transaction occurred as of an earlier date, nor are they indicative of operating results and financial position that may occur in the future. Except where used to extinguish the nonrecourse debt collateralized by credit card receivables, the unaudited pro forma consolidated financial statements do not reflect the anticipated use of the net cash proceeds, including share repurchases and additional debt extinguishments. As a result, the unaudited pro forma Consolidated Statements of Operations do not reflect anticipated favorable impacts on interest expense and earnings per share. The unaudited pro forma consolidated financial statements should be read in conjunction with the historical consolidated financial statements and notes thereto in the Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K for the fiscal year ended January&nbsp;28, 2012 and the Quarterly Report on Form&nbsp;10-Q for the quarter ended October&nbsp;27, 2012.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 27.35pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(a)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Removes finance charge revenue, late fee revenue and third-party merchant fees.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.05pt;text-indent:-27.35pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 27.35pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(b)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Reflects the net impact of the profit sharing arrangement with TD ($742 million), ongoing expenses ($288 million) and the reduction of the beneficial interest asset ($55 million).&#160; The amount of the reduction of the beneficial interest asset is based on actual 2011 payment patterns, which we do not expect to reflect future payment patterns.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.05pt;text-indent:-27.35pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 27.35pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(c)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Eliminates bad debt expense ($154 million) and reclassifies ongoing expenses to selling, general and administrative expenses ($292 million).</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.05pt;text-indent:-27.35pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 27.35pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(d)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Eliminates interest expense related to the nonrecourse debt collateralized by credit card receivables, which was extinguished concurrent with the close of the transaction.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.05pt;text-indent:-27.35pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 27.35pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(e)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Income tax impact of adjustments.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(a)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Removes finance charge revenue, late fee revenue and third-party merchant fees.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(b)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Reflects the net impact of the profit sharing arrangement with TD ($579 million), ongoing expenses ($198 million) and the reduction of the beneficial interest asset ($54 million).</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(c)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Eliminates bad debt expense ($141 million) and reclassifies ongoing expenses to selling, general and administrative expenses ($192 million).</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(d)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Historically, our credit card receivables were recorded at par value less an allowance for doubtful accounts. In the third quarter of 2012, our receivables were classified as held for sale and recorded at the lower of cost (par) or fair value, resulting in a gain of $156 million. The gain on receivables held for sale is eliminated for this pro forma presentation.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(e)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Eliminates interest expense related to the nonrecourse debt collateralized by credit card receivables, which was extinguished concurrent with the close of the transaction.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(f)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Income tax impact of adjustments.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(a)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Cash proceeds resulting from an assumed transaction close on October&nbsp;27, 2012 ($5.8 billion), offset by the concurrent paydown of nonrecourse debt ($1.5 billion) and transaction costs paid associated with the sale of receivables ($12 million).</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(b)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Eliminates credit card receivables sold.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(c)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Records the current portion of the beneficial interest asset recognized at close ($107 million), current deferred income tax assets ($33 million) and other miscellaneous adjustments.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(d)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Records the long-term portion of the beneficial interest asset.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(e)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Records the impact to income tax liabilities.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(f)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Removes nonrecourse debt collateralized by credit card receivables that was paid down concurrent with close.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(g)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Gain resulting from the transaction, net of taxes.</font></i></p>

  </head>
<body lang="EN-US">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit (2)G</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">EXECUTION COPY</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FIRST AMENDMENT TO PURCHASE AND SALE AGREEMENT</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">This FIRST AMENDMENT TO PURCHASE AND SALE AGREEMENT (hereinafter the &#147;Amendment&#148;) is made as of the 13</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;position:relative;top:-4.0pt;">th</font>&#160;day of March, 2013 (&#147;Effective Date&#148;), by and among Target National Bank, a national banking association,&#160; Target Receivables LLC, a Minnesota limited liability company, Target Corporation, a Minnesota corporation, and TD Bank USA, N.A., a national banking association.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">WHEREAS, the parties have previously entered into that certain Purchase and Sale Agreement dated October&nbsp;22, 2012 (the &#147;Agreement&#148;); and</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">WHEREAS, the parties desire to amend the Agreement as set forth herein;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">NOW, THEREFORE,&nbsp;In consideration of the foregoing premises and mutual covenants hereinafter set forth, the parties agree as follows:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The definitions of &#147;Deposit Account Agreement&#148; and &#147;Pledge and Security Agreement&#148; set forth in Section&nbsp;1.1 of the Agreement are hereby deleted in their entirety and replaced with the following:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#147;<u>Deposit Account Agreement</u>&#148; means both of Deposit Account Agreement #1 and Deposit Account Agreement #2, each by and between Target National Bank and Target Corporation, and each dated as of April&nbsp;28, 2009, true and correct copies of which are attached hereto as <u>Exhibit&nbsp;C-1</u> and<u> Exhibit&nbsp;C-2</u> respectively.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#147;<u>Pledge and Security Agreement</u>&#148; means both of the Pledge and Security Agreements dated as of April&nbsp;28, 2009, by and between Target National Bank and Target Corporation.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The definition of &#147;Permissible Liens&#148; set forth in Section&nbsp;1.1 of the Agreement is hereby deleted in its entirety and replaced with the following:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#147;<u>Permissible Liens</u>&#148; means Liens for Taxes not yet due and payable and those Liens created or evidenced by the financing statements described in <u>Schedule N</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Section&nbsp;3.1(d)&nbsp;of the Agreement is hereby deleted in its entirety and replaced with the following:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Subject to the following provisions of this subsection 3.1(d), the Purchaser agrees to assume all rights and obligations of Target National Bank under the Deposit Account Agreement, including all Deposit Liabilities thereunder to the extent outstanding as of the Closing Date.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">(i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; On the Closing Date, the Sellers shall pay to the Purchaser the estimated amount of the Deposit Liabilities held by Target National Bank for the Parent as of the Closing Date, as reflected on the Estimated Closing </font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Statement (which payment shall be made by a deduction from the Purchase Price).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">(ii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; On the Business Day following the Closing Date, the Purchaser shall pay to the depositor the same estimated amount of such Deposit Liabilities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">(iii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; If the estimated Deposit Liabilities paid to the Purchaser on the Closing Date pursuant to subsection (i), above, are less than the actual Deposit Liabilities assumed by Purchaser as reflected on the Final Closing Statement, the remaining balance due from the Sellers to the Purchaser for the assumed Deposit Liabilities shall be offset against the amount due from the Purchaser to the depositor for the same remaining balance of the assumed Deposit Liabilities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">(iv)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; If the estimated Deposit Liabilities paid to the Purchaser on the Closing Date pursuant to subsection (i), above, exceed the actual Deposit Liabilities assumed by Purchaser as reflected on the Final Closing Statement, the excess amount paid by the Sellers to the Purchaser for the overestimated assumed Deposit Liabilities shall be offset against excess amount paid by the Purchaser to the depositor pursuant to subsection (ii), above, for the same overestimated assumed Deposit Liabilities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-align:justify;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The form of Estimated Closing Statement attached to the Agreement as Schedule A is hereby replaced with the form of Estimated Closing Statement attached hereto as <u>Schedule A</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The form of Final Closing Statement attached to the Agreement as Schedule B is hereby replaced with the form of Final Closing Statement attached hereto as <u>Schedule B</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Schedule N</u> attached to this Amendment is hereby attached to the Agreement as <u>Schedule N</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Form&nbsp;of Instrument of Assignment and Assumption attached to the Agreement as Annex A is hereby replaced with the Form&nbsp;of Instrument of Assignment and Assumption attached hereto as <u>Annex A</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Exhibit&nbsp;C attached to the Agreement is relabeled as <u>Exhibit&nbsp;C-1</u> and <u>Exhibit&nbsp;C-2</u> attached to this Amendment is attached to the Agreement as <u>Exhibit&nbsp;C-2</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All terms and conditions of the Agreement not specifically modified in this Amendment shall remain unchanged and in full force and effect.</p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit (99)</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-weight:bold;"><img width="59" height="71" src="g71241mmi001.jpg"></font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">

<td width="17%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:17.26%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">John Hulbert,&nbsp;Investors, (612) 761-6627</font></p>    </td>   </tr>

<td width="17%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:17.26%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Stacey Wempen, Financial Media, (612) 761-6785</font></p>    </td>   </tr>

<td width="17%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:17.26%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="82%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:82.76%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Target Media Hotline,   (612) 696-3400</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="4" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Target Announces Closing of</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="4" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:14.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Credit Card Portfolio Sale to TD Bank Group</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="4" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:14.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;line-height:150%;">MINNEAPOLIS (March&nbsp;13, 2013) </font></b>&#151; Target Corporation (NYSE:TGT) announced today that it has completed the sale of its entire consumer credit card portfolio to TD Bank Group (TSX and NYSE: TD) for $5.7 billion, the gross value of the outstanding receivables (&#147;par&#148;) at the time of closing. As previously announced, the two companies have entered into a seven-year program agreement under which TD will also underwrite, fund and own future Target Credit Card and Target Visa receivables in the United States. Under the program agreement, TD will control risk management policies and oversee regulatory compliance and Target will continue to perform account servicing functions.</p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">&#147;We&#146;re pleased that we&#146;ve completed the sale of our credit card portfolio,&#148; said Gregg Steinhafel, chairman, president and chief executive officer of Target Corporation. &#147;We look forward to working with TD Bank Group, a premier financial institution, to provide innovative financial products to our guests and profitably grow the portfolio over time.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Under the seven-year program agreement, which applies to Target&#146;s U.S. credit card operations, Target will maintain the current deep integration between its financial services operations and its retail operations. The agreement does not have any impact on Target&#146;s 5% REDcard Rewards program. Target team members will continue to provide all servicing for Target Credit Card and Target Visa accounts. The portfolio sale and program agreement are designed to have minimal impact on Target&#146;s current cardholders, guests and the Target team members who support financial products and services.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#150; more &#150;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-style:italic;">Target Announces Closing the Sale of its Credit Card Portfolio to TD &#150; Page&nbsp;</font></i><i><font style="font-style:italic;">2</font> of 4</i><a name="PB_2_041217_141"></a></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;line-height:150%;">Accounting Considerations, Earnings Impacts and Deployment of Proceeds</font></b></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">As previously announced, Target&#146;s fiscal 2012 GAAP earnings per share reflected a pre-tax gain of $161 million related to the accounting treatment of the consumer credit card receivables as &#147;held for sale&#148; assets. In addition, in first quarter 2013 Target estimates it will recognize an additional pre-tax gain of approximately $393 million on the sale of its portfolio. At the time of the company&#146;s October&nbsp;23, 2012 announcement of the sale agreement with TD, Target posted details on the accounting aspects of this transaction on its investor relations website, available at <u>www.Target.com/investors</u>.</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Target expects to deploy proceeds from the sale in a manner that will preserve its strong investment-grade credit ratings. Specifically, the company expects to apply approximately 90 percent of net transaction proceeds to reduce the company&#146;s net debt position, with the remainder applied to share repurchase over time. Concurrent with this release Target announced that it has commenced tender offers to apply cash proceeds of up to $1.2 billion to retire certain long-term debt securities.</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Under the terms of the program agreement, Target will continue to earn a substantial portion of the profits generated by the credit card portfolio. Beginning with first quarter 2013, Target will no longer report a Credit Card segment and the income from the profit-sharing arrangement, net of account servicing expenses, will be recognized as an offset to SG&amp;A expense in a new U.S. Segment.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#150; more &#150;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-style:italic;">Target Announces Closing the Sale of its Credit Card Portfolio to TD &#150; Page&nbsp;</font></i><i><font style="font-style:italic;">3</font> of 4</i><a name="PB_3_041217_7608"></a></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Target continues to expect that net income from the portfolio profit-sharing arrangement, combined with the benefit of debt reduction and share repurchase resulting from deployment of proceeds from the sale, will result in mild dilution to Target&#146;s adjusted earnings per share in the first 12 months following closing*. Specifically, Target expects that in the 12 months following closing its adjusted earnings per share will be approximately 10 cents lower compared with a scenario in which Target continued to fund its portfolio. Based on its forecast for income from profit sharing combined with the expected benefit from share repurchase and interest savings, Target expects that the adjusted EPS impact of this transaction will become neutral over time. The company expects to provide additional detail on the impact of the sale and debt tender offers on its 2013 financial results following final settlement of the debt tender offers, which is expected to occur in first quarter 2013.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-left:none;border-right:none;border-top:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:1.0pt 0in 1.0pt 0in;">
<p style="border:none;line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;padding:0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:2.0pt;line-height:150%;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;padding:0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">*Target calculates adjusted earnings per share to measure the results from operations in its U.S. businesses. Accordingly, adjusted earnings per share excludes the impact of Target&#146;s Canadian Segment and other non-segment expenses related to its Canadian market entry.</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;padding:0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:2.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
</div>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;line-height:150%;">Miscellaneous</font></b></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">For additional details on Target&#146;s credit card portfolio transaction with TD please refer to Target&#146;s October&nbsp;23, 2012 press release, which is available on the company&#146;s website at <u>www.Target.com/investors</u>.</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Statements in this release related to the deployment of proceeds and the transaction&#146;s expected impact on earnings performance are forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. Such statements speak only as of the date they are made and are subject to risks and uncertainties&nbsp;which could cause&nbsp;the company&#146;s&nbsp;actual results&nbsp;to differ materially.&nbsp;The most important risks and uncertainties are described in&nbsp;Item 1A&nbsp;of the company&#146;s&nbsp;Form&nbsp;10-K for the fiscal year ended January&nbsp;28, 2012 and Form&nbsp;10-Q for the fiscal quarter ended July&nbsp;28, 2012.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#150; more &#150;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-style:italic;">Target Announces Closing the Sale of its Credit Card Portfolio to TD &#150; Page&nbsp;</font></i><i><font style="font-style:italic;">4</font> of 4</i><a name="PB_4_041217_8146"></a></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Target</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Minneapolis-based Target Corporation (NYSE: TGT) serves guests at 1,787 stores &#150; 1,784 in the United States and three in Canada -- and at Target.com. Since 1946, Target has given 5 percent of its profit through community grants and programs; today, that giving equals more than $4 million a week. For more information about Target&#146;s commitment to corporate responsibility, visit <u>Target.com/corporateresponsibility</u>.</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="line-height:150%;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">For more information, visit <u>Target.com/Pressroom</u>.</font></p>
